## 🔍 Cross-Page Patterns: Common HTML Issues

These HTML patterns cause the same accessibility errors across multiple pages. **Fix the pattern once in your codebase to fix it everywhere!**

### 🎯 Top Patterns to Fix (Highest Impact)

#### Pattern 1: Affects 87 page(s) - 522 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: ALFA
**Rule**: [SIA-R3: lang attribute has a valid language code](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r3)
**Issue**: The element does not have a unique ID

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<ul class="ppg-menu__list-2l" tabindex="0" id="submenu_principal" role="menubar">...</ul>
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
/ul[@id="submenu_principal"]
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('/ul[@id="submenu_principal"]')`
5. The element will be highlighted

**Affected Pages**:
- https://administracion.gob.es/
- https://administracion.gob.es/pag_Home
- https://administracion.gob.es/pag_Home/Tu-espacio-europeo/derechos-obligaciones/ciudadanos/asistencia-sanitaria/centros-atencion-sociosanitaria
- https://administracion.gob.es/pag_Home/Tu-espacio-europeo/derechos-obligaciones/ciudadanos/asistencia-sanitaria/estancia-TSE
- https://administracion.gob.es/pag_Home/Tu-espacio-europeo/derechos-obligaciones/ciudadanos/asistencia-sanitaria/numeros-urgencia

## Detailed Failure Information (ALFA)

### https://administracion.gob.es/

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a data-fn="rrss" href="#ni" class="ppg-link ppg-link--header">Contacto</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="ppg-link ppg-link--header"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="ppg-link ppg-link--btn" target="_blank" href="https://sede.administracion.gob.es/carpeta">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="ppg-link ppg-link--btn"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button type="button" data-role="none" class="slick-prev slick-arrow slick-disabled" role="button" aria-disabled="true" style="">Anterior</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="slick-prev slick-arrow slick-disabled"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<ul class="slick-slide slick-current slick-active" data-slick-index="0" aria-hidden="false" tabindex="-1" role="option" aria-describedby="slick-slide00">...</ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@class="slick-slide slick-current slick-active"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<ul class="slick-slide slick-active" data-slick-index="1" aria-hidden="false" tabindex="-1" role="option" aria-describedby="slick-slide01">...</ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@class="slick-slide slick-active"]`

*... and 10 more failures for this rule*

#### Rule: [SIA-R113](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r113)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size and spacing
- HTML: `<ul class="slick-slide slick-current slick-active" data-slick-index="0" aria-hidden="false" tabindex="-1" role="option" aria-describedby="slick-slide00">...</ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@class="slick-slide slick-current slick-active"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size and spacing
- HTML: `<ul class="slick-slide slick-active" data-slick-index="1" aria-hidden="false" tabindex="-1" role="option" aria-describedby="slick-slide01">...</ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@class="slick-slide slick-active"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R2: HTML elements have a valid lang attribute](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r2)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The image does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<img class="fullImg" alt=" " title=" " src="/dam/jcr:e31ce16e-02c8-487e-b5dc-8163515b1293/oficina-atencion.jpg" />`
- XPath: `/img[@class="fullImg"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R3: lang attribute has a valid language code](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r3)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<ul class="ppg-menu__list-2l" tabindex="0" id="submenu_principal" role="menubar">...</ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@id="submenu_principal"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R53: Headings follow a logical hierarchy](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r53)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The heading skips one or more levels
- HTML: `<h3 class="o-card__title ppg-heading t-fs-18">Novedades de información para personas afectadas p...</h3>`
- XPath: `/h3[@class="o-card__title ppg-heading t-fs-18"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R57: Landmarks don't repeat the same content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r57)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The text is not included in a landmark region

#### Rule: [SIA-R66: Text has enhanced contrast with its background](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r66)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 5.51:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

#### Rule: [SIA-R71](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r71)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The text of the paragraph is justified
- HTML: `<p class="textojustificado">Un informe de AESAN detalla hábitos alimentarios p...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="textojustificado"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is `normal` which will result in a line height of less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="o-card__link ppg-icon__crossR-2a ppg-link">TE AYUDAMOS</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="o-card__link ppg-icon__crossR-2a ppg-link"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="o-card__text ppg-text ppg-text--lighted-2">Publicadas las fiestas laborales para el año 2026.</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="o-card__text ppg-text ppg-text--lighted-2"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="txt_alignR">...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="txt_alignR"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="ppg-text t-margin-bottom-15">Acceso directo a servicios electrónicos frecuentes</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="ppg-text t-margin-bottom-15"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="textojustificado">Información práctica, fiable y de calidad para la ...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="textojustificado"]`

*... and 4 more failures for this rule*

#### Rule: [SIA-R74](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r74)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="o-card__text ppg-text ppg-text--lighted-2">Publicadas las fiestas laborales para el año 2026.</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="o-card__text ppg-text ppg-text--lighted-2"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p>Consulta la información y las medidas que se van p...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="txt_alignR">...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="txt_alignR"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="textojustificado">Un informe de AESAN detalla hábitos alimentarios p...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="textojustificado"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="ppg-text t-margin-bottom-15">Acceso directo a servicios electrónicos frecuentes</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="ppg-text t-margin-bottom-15"]`

*... and 3 more failures for this rule*

#### Rule: [SIA-R8: Form elements have accessible labels](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r8)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The form field does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<div class="slick-track" role="listbox" style="opacity: 1; width: 20000px; transform: translate3d(0px, 0px, 0px);">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@class="slick-track"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R80: ASCII art has a text alternative](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r80)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p title="Atención e información" class="ppg-menu__link" tabindex="0">...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="ppg-menu__link"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The line height is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p>Consulta la información y las medidas que se van p...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The line height is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="txt_alignR">...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="txt_alignR"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The line height is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="textojustificado">Un informe de AESAN detalla hábitos alimentarios p...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="textojustificado"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R90: iframe elements have an accessible name](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r90)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element has tabbable descendants
- HTML: `<ul class="slick-slide slick-current slick-active" data-slick-index="0" aria-hidden="false" tabindex="-1" role="option" aria-describedby="slick-slide00">...</ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@class="slick-slide slick-current slick-active"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The element has tabbable descendants
- HTML: `<ul class="slick-slide slick-active" data-slick-index="1" aria-hidden="false" tabindex="-1" role="option" aria-describedby="slick-slide01">...</ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@class="slick-slide slick-active"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The element has tabbable descendants
- HTML: `<ul class="slick-slide slick-current slick-active slick-center" data-slick-index="0" aria-hidden="false" tabindex="-1" role="option" aria-describedby="slick-slide10">...</ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@class="slick-slide slick-current slick-active slick-center"]`

- HTML: `<a data-fn="rrss" href="#ni" class="ppg-link ppg-link--header">Contacto</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="ppg-link ppg-link--header"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="ppg-link ppg-link--btn" target="_blank" href="https://sede.administracion.gob.es/carpeta">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="ppg-link ppg-link--btn"]`

**Failure 3:**

- HTML: `<a class="t-fs-16" href="/pag_Home/index.html" title="Punto de Acceso General">                           Inicio                 ...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="t-fs-16"]`

**Failure 4:**

- XPath: `/a`

- XPath: `/a[@class="lnk_arriba disabled"]`

- XPath: `/p[@class="textojustificado"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p>...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="txt_alignR">...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="txt_alignR"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="ppg-text ppg-text--top-lighted">Directorate-General of Public Governance</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="ppg-text ppg-text--top-lighted"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="ppg-text t-fs-10">Unión Europea  Fondo Europeo de Desarrollo Regiona...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="ppg-text t-fs-10"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R78: Headings of same level have text content between them](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r78)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: There is no content between this heading and the next
- HTML: `<h3 class="subtitulo"> </h3>`
- XPath: `/h3[@class="subtitulo"]`

- HTML: `<p class="textojustificado">Todos los consumidores tienen derecho a conectarse...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="textojustificado"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="txt_alignR">...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="txt_alignR"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="parrafoLista">El enganche: la operación de acoplar la instalació...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="parrafoLista"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p>...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="ppg-text ppg-text--top-lighted">Dirección General de Gobernanza Pública</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="ppg-text ppg-text--top-lighted"]`

- HTML: `<p class="textojustificado">Los Regímenes Especiales de los Funcionarios Públi...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="textojustificado"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="txt_alignR">...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="txt_alignR"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="ppg-text ppg-text--top-lighted">Dirección General de Gobernanza Pública</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="ppg-text ppg-text--top-lighted"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p>...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="ppg-text t-fs-10">Unión Europea  Fondo Europeo de Desarrollo Regiona...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="ppg-text t-fs-10"]`

- HTML: `<p class="textojustificado">Para poder votar en las elecciones europeas es nec...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="textojustificado"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="txt_alignR">...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="txt_alignR"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="ppg-text ppg-text--top-lighted">Dirección General de Gobernanza Pública</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="ppg-text ppg-text--top-lighted"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p>...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="ppg-text t-fs-10">Unión Europea  Fondo Europeo de Desarrollo Regiona...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="ppg-text t-fs-10"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R80: ASCII art has a text alternative](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r80)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p title="Atención e información" class="ppg-menu__link" tabindex="0">...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="ppg-menu__link"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The line height is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="textojustificado">Para poder votar en las elecciones europeas es nec...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="textojustificado"]`

**Failure 3:**

- HTML: `<p class="txt_alignR">...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="txt_alignR"]`

- HTML: `<p>...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

- HTML: `<p title="Atención e información" class="ppg-menu__link" tabindex="0">...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="ppg-menu__link"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The line height is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="txt_alignR">...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="txt_alignR"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The line height is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p>...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

- HTML: `<a class="ppg-link ppg-link--btn" target="_blank" href="https://sede.administracion.gob.es/carpeta">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="ppg-link ppg-link--btn"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button type="button" data-role="none" class="slick-prev slick-arrow slick-disabled" role="button" aria-disabled="true" style="">Anterior</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="slick-prev slick-arrow slick-disabled"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<ul class="slick-slide slick-current slick-active" data-slick-index="0" aria-hidden="false" tabindex="-1" role="option" aria-describedby="slick-slide00">...</ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@class="slick-slide slick-current slick-active"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<ul class="slick-slide slick-active" data-slick-index="1" aria-hidden="false" tabindex="-1" role="option" aria-describedby="slick-slide01">...</ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@class="slick-slide slick-active"]`

*... and 10 more failures for this rule*

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="o-card__text ppg-text ppg-text--lighted-2">Publicades les festes laborals per a l'any 2023</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="o-card__text ppg-text ppg-text--lighted-2"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is `normal` which will result in a line height of less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="o-card__link ppg-icon__crossR-2a ppg-link">Informa't</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="o-card__link ppg-icon__crossR-2a ppg-link"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="txt_alignR">...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="txt_alignR"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="ppg-text t-margin-bottom-15">Accés directe a servicis electrònics freqüents</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="ppg-text t-margin-bottom-15"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="textojustificado">Informaci&oacute;n pr&aacute;ctica, fiable y de ca...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="textojustificado"]`

- XPath: `/p[@class="ppg-text t-fs-10"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p>...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p>...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

**Failure 3:**

- HTML: `<p class="ppg-text t-fs-10">Unión Europea  Fondo Europeo de Desarrollo Regiona...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="ppg-text t-fs-10"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)

- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="textojustificado">La presentación electrónica de ofertas supone que ...</p>`

**Failure 2:**

- XPath: `/p[@class="ppg-text t-fs-10"]`

## Detailed Failure Information (axe)

### https://administracion.gob.es/

#### Rule: [aria-allowed-role](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-allowed-role?application=playwright)
**Impact**: minor

**Failure 1:**
- Message: ARIA role should be appropriate for the element
- HTML: `<ul class="slick-slide slick-current slick-active" data-slick-index="0" aria-hidden="false" tabindex="-1" role="option" aria-describedby="slick-slide00">`
- XPath: `ul[aria-describedby="slick-slide00"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: ARIA role should be appropriate for the element
- HTML: `<ul class="slick-slide slick-active" data-slick-index="1" aria-hidden="false" tabindex="-1" role="option" aria-describedby="slick-slide01">`
- XPath: `ul[aria-describedby="slick-slide01"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: ARIA role should be appropriate for the element
- HTML: `<ul class="slick-slide slick-active" data-slick-index="2" aria-hidden="false" tabindex="-1" role="option" aria-describedby="slick-slide02">`
- XPath: `ul[aria-describedby="slick-slide02"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: ARIA role should be appropriate for the element
- HTML: `<a href="#tab-0" class="ppg-tabs__link ui-tabs-anchor" role="presentation" tabindex="-1" id="ui-id-1">Servicios ELECTRÓNICOS frecuentes</a>`
- XPath: `#ui-id-1`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: ARIA role should be appropriate for the element
- HTML: `<ul class="slick-slide slick-current slick-active slick-center" data-slick-index="0" aria-hidden="false" tabindex="-1" role="option" aria-describedby="slick-slide10">`
- XPath: `ul[aria-describedby="slick-slide10"]`

*... and 2 more failures for this rule*

#### Rule: [aria-input-field-name](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-input-field-name?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious

**Failure 1:**
- Message: ARIA input fields must have an accessible name
- HTML: `<div class="slick-track" role="listbox" style="opacity: 1; width: 20000px; transform: translate3d(0px, 0px, 0px);">`
- XPath: `.ppg-slick--type1 > .slick-list.draggable[aria-live="polite"] > .slick-track[role="listbox"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: ARIA input fields must have an accessible name
- HTML: `<div class="slick-track" role="listbox" style="opacity: 1; width: 55000px; transform: translate3d(-600px, 0px, 0px);">`
- XPath: `div[data-fn="slick-type2"] > .slick-list.draggable[aria-live="polite"] > .slick-track[role="listbox"]`

#### Rule: [aria-required-children](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-required-children?application=playwright)
**Impact**: critical

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Certain ARIA roles must contain particular children
- HTML: `<div class="slick-track" role="listbox" style="opacity: 1; width: 55000px; transform: translate3d(-600px, 0px, 0px);">`
- XPath: `div[data-fn="slick-type2"] > .slick-list.draggable[aria-live="polite"] > .slick-track[role="listbox"]`

#### Rule: [aria-toggle-field-name](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-toggle-field-name?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious

**Failure 1:**
- Message: ARIA toggle fields must have an accessible name
- HTML: `<ul class="slick-slide slick-active" data-slick-index="1" aria-hidden="false" tabindex="-1" role="option" aria-describedby="slick-slide11">`
- XPath: `ul[aria-describedby="slick-slide11"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: ARIA toggle fields must have an accessible name
- HTML: `<ul class="slick-slide slick-active" data-slick-index="2" aria-hidden="false" tabindex="-1" role="option" aria-describedby="slick-slide12">`
- XPath: `ul[aria-describedby="slick-slide12"]`

#### Rule: [heading-order](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/heading-order?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Heading levels should only increase by one
- HTML: `<h3 class="o-card__title ppg-heading t-fs-18">Novedades de información para personas afectadas por la DANA </h3>`
- XPath: `ul[aria-describedby="slick-slide00"] > .ppg-slick__item > .ppg-slick__link[title=""][target="_blank"] > .o-card--slick.o-card > .o-card__content > .t-fs-18.o-card__title`

#### Rule: [image-alt](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/image-alt?application=playwright)
**Impact**: critical

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Images must have alternative text
- HTML: `<img class="fullImg" alt=" " title=" " src="/dam/jcr:e31ce16e-02c8-487e-b5dc-8163515b1293/oficina-atencion.jpg">`
- XPath: `.fullImg`

#### Rule: [label-title-only](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/label-title-only?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Form elements should have a visible label
- HTML: `<input type="text" name="q" id="buscador-header" maxlength="150" title="Buscar" placeholder="Buscar" class="ppg-search__input ppg-text ppg-text--lighted ppg-icon__search-ra" onfocus="javascript:this.value=''">`
- XPath: `#buscador-header`

#### Rule: [listitem](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/listitem?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious

**Failure 1:**
- Message: <li> elements must be contained in a <ul> or <ol>
- HTML: `<li class="ppg-slick__item">`
- XPath: `ul[aria-describedby="slick-slide00"] > .ppg-slick__item`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: <li> elements must be contained in a <ul> or <ol>
- HTML: `<li class="ppg-slick__item">`
- XPath: `ul[aria-describedby="slick-slide01"] > .ppg-slick__item`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: <li> elements must be contained in a <ul> or <ol>
- HTML: `<li class="ppg-slick__item">`
- XPath: `ul[aria-describedby="slick-slide02"] > .ppg-slick__item`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: <li> elements must be contained in a <ul> or <ol>
- HTML: `<li class="ppg-slick__item">`
- XPath: `ul[aria-describedby="slick-slide10"] > .ppg-slick__item`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: <li> elements must be contained in a <ul> or <ol>
- HTML: `<li class="ppg-slick__item">`
- XPath: `ul[aria-describedby="slick-slide11"] > .ppg-slick__item`

*... and 1 more failures for this rule*

#### Rule: [nested-interactive](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/nested-interactive?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Interactive controls must not be nested
- HTML: `<ul class="slick-slide slick-current slick-active" data-slick-index="0" aria-hidden="false" tabindex="-1" role="option" aria-describedby="slick-slide00">`
- XPath: `ul[aria-describedby="slick-slide00"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Interactive controls must not be nested
- HTML: `<ul class="slick-slide slick-active" data-slick-index="1" aria-hidden="false" tabindex="-1" role="option" aria-describedby="slick-slide01">`
- XPath: `ul[aria-describedby="slick-slide01"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Interactive controls must not be nested
- HTML: `<ul class="slick-slide slick-active" data-slick-index="2" aria-hidden="false" tabindex="-1" role="option" aria-describedby="slick-slide02">`
- XPath: `ul[aria-describedby="slick-slide02"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Interactive controls must not be nested
- HTML: `<li class="ppg-tabs__item ui-tabs-tab ui-corner-top ui-state-default ui-tab ui-tabs-active ui-state-active" role="tab" tabindex="0" aria-controls="tab-0" aria-labelledby="ui-id-1" aria-selected="true" aria-expanded="true">`
- XPath: `.ppg-tabs__item`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Interactive controls must not be nested
- HTML: `<ul class="slick-slide slick-current slick-active slick-center" data-slick-index="0" aria-hidden="false" tabindex="-1" role="option" aria-describedby="slick-slide10">`
- XPath: `ul[aria-describedby="slick-slide10"]`

#### Rule: [presentation-role-conflict](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/presentation-role-conflict?application=playwright)
**Impact**: minor

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Elements marked as presentational should be consistently ignored
- HTML: `<a href="#tab-0" class="ppg-tabs__link ui-tabs-anchor" role="presentation" tabindex="-1" id="ui-id-1">Servicios ELECTRÓNICOS frecuentes</a>`
- XPath: `#ui-id-1`

#### Rule: [region](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/region?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: All page content should be contained by landmarks
- HTML: `<div>`
- XPath: `#general_content > div:nth-child(3)`

### https://administracion.gob.es/pag_Home

#### Rule: [aria-allowed-role](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-allowed-role?application=playwright)

- Message: ARIA role should be appropriate for the element
- HTML: `<ul class="slick-slide slick-current slick-active" data-slick-index="0" aria-hidden="false" tabindex="-1" role="option" aria-describedby="slick-slide00">`
- XPath: `ul[aria-describedby="slick-slide00"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: ARIA role should be appropriate for the element
- HTML: `<ul class="slick-slide slick-active" data-slick-index="1" aria-hidden="false" tabindex="-1" role="option" aria-describedby="slick-slide01">`
- XPath: `ul[aria-describedby="slick-slide01"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: ARIA role should be appropriate for the element
- HTML: `<ul class="slick-slide slick-active" data-slick-index="2" aria-hidden="false" tabindex="-1" role="option" aria-describedby="slick-slide02">`
- XPath: `ul[aria-describedby="slick-slide02"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: ARIA role should be appropriate for the element

- XPath: `#ui-id-1`
